# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kafka Connect REST API v1 to v2 Migration

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the Kafka Connect REST API: the v1 connector resource handlers, the v2 connector resource handlers, and the version routing logic. Identify what changed between v1 and v2 in the task status and error response schemas.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

95-assistanttext-
I've successfully compiled a comprehensive analysis of the Kafka Connect REST API implementation in Apache Kafka. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Key Findings

**Main REST API Resource Handler:**
- `ConnectorsResource.java` - Primary JAX-RS resource handler for all connector management endpoints

**Response Schema Classes:**
1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java** - Defines TaskState and ConnectorState classes with fields:
   - TaskState: id, state, worker_id, msg (trace), version
   - ConnectorState: state, worker_id, msg, version

2. **ErrorMessage.java** - Standard error response format with error_code and message

3. **TaskInfo.java** - Task configuration entity

**Error Handling:**
- `ConnectExceptionMapper.java` - Maps exceptions to ErrorMessage responses with appropriate HTTP status codes

**Version Routing & Configuration:**
- `ConnectRestServer.java` - Registers REST resources
- `RestServer.java` - Base REST server implementation

**Schema Versioning Evidence:**
- **KafkaConfigBackingStore.java** contains:
  - `TARGET_STATE_V0`: Only "state" field
  - `TARGET_STATE_V1`: Adds optional "state.v2" field (backward compatible)

This represents the v0 to v1 schema evolution, where v1 adds support for new state values while maintaining backward compatibility.

The results have been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with detailed documentation of all relevant files, symbols, and the complete request/response chain architecture.

ErrorMessage (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ErrorMessage.java) - Standard error response with error_code (int) and message (String) fields.\\n\\n3. TaskInfo (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/TaskInfo.java) - Contains task identifier and configuration map.\\n\\nError response generation is handled by ConnectExceptionMapper (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectExceptionMapper.java), which maps exceptions to ErrorMessage responses with appropriate HTTP status codes.\\n\\nVersion routing and REST server configuration is managed by:\\n- ConnectRestServer (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java) - Extends RestServer to register all REST resources\\n- RestServer (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/RestServer.java) - Base REST server implementation that registers resource handlers\\n\\nSchema versioning is evident in KafkaConfigBackingStore.java (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/storage/KafkaConfigBackingStore.java) where:\\n- TARGET_STATE_V0: Contains only \\\"state\\\" field (String)\\n- TARGET_STATE_V1: Adds optional \\\"state.v2\\\" field for new state values\\n\\nThis represents schema evolution from v0 to v1 for target state storage. The v1 schema maintains backward compatibility by making the new state.v2 field optional, allowing clients to work with the new field while older instances continue using the state field.\\n\\nThe request flow: HTTP Request -> ConnectorsResource methods -> Herder interface -> ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState response -> ErrorMessage for errors.\\n\\nNote: The codebase does not show separate v1 and v2 REST API endpoint classes.
